Welcome fruit twice a day, use Dyson for hair dryer. Rich content. The parent-child slides and dolls in the room make children do not want to go out.

Children also feel that it is too cold. Generally, it is more appropriate to adjust it to 29 to 30 degrees.

Overall, the price is still very high. If the National Day can go to Shanghai, I will come to play. No wonder our company chose this hotel as an agreement hotel. It is definitely a good place for winter and summer vacations, and the best choice for business trips near Xiaoshan!
